The Company currently estimates its second half 2015 GAAP operating revenues will increase approximately $400 million from the combined impact of the amended agreement and the effect of a change in accounting methodology</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">4</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gary C. Kelly, Chairman of the Board, President, and Chief Executive Officer, stated, "We are delighted to report another strong quarter of earnings. Our net income, excluding special items, of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">691 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.03</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, is an all-time quarterly high and represents our ninth consecutive quarter of record profits.&#160;Operating income, excluding special&#160;items, increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">40.2</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent year-over-year, producing a strong </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">22.5</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent operating margin. We significantly expanded our margins and generated very strong cash flows during first half 2015, allowing us to return $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">811 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to Shareholders through dividends and share repurchases so far this year. In addition, we intend to launch a $500 million accelerated share repurchase program soon.&#160;We have a solid investment grade balance </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">sheet, and we are pleased with the recent upgrade to Baa1 by Moody's.&#160;For first half 2015, our record profits have earned our outstanding Employees a record $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">308 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;profitsharing accrual, nearly doubling first half 2014&#8217;s contribution. For the 12 months ended June 30, 2015, our ROIC was an outstanding </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">28.2</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent, far surpassing our cost of capital. Our 2015 results, thus far, are exceptional, and our current outlook for the second half of 2015 is also strong, laying a solid foundation to surpass 2014's ROIC.&#160; </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Fuel savings</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">5</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in second quarter 2015 were nearly $500 million, which led to a reduction in our second quarter 2015 unit costs, excluding special items, of almost 12 percent year-over-year.&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;economic fuel costs were $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2.02</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per gallon, compared with $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3.02</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per gallon in </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. Based on our existing fuel derivative contracts and market prices as of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">July&#160;20, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, we expect significant year-over-year fuel savings again in third quarter 2015, with economic fuel costs currently estimated to be approximately $2.20 per gallon, as compared with third quarter 2014's $2.94 per gallon. </font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;We also were very pleased with our overall cost performance. Our cost control efforts, ongoing fleet modernization, and improved aircraft utilization resulted in a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.8</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent year-over-year decline in our second quarter 2015 unit costs, excluding fuel and oil expense, special items, and second quarter 2015's record profitsharing expense of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">182 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. Based on current cost trends, and excluding fuel and oil expense, special items, and profitsharing, we expect third quarter 2015 unit costs to decline approximately one percent and full year 2015 unit costs to decline approximately two percent, both compared with the same year-ago periods. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;Our second quarter 2015 operating unit revenue performance was impacted by challenging year-over-year comparisons, longer average stage length, higher average seats per trip (gauge), and a softer yield environment. Still, we grew second quarter 2015 operating revenues </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2.0</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent to a record $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">5.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;on a year-over-year increase in available seat miles (ASMs) of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">7.0</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent. Demand for our popular low fares remained strong throughout the quarter resulting in a record </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">84.6</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent load factor. Our second quarter 2015 unit revenues declined </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">4.7</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent, as expected, driven largely by the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">5.4</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent decline in passenger revenue yields, both as compared with second quarter last year. The year-ago results included $47 million in additional passenger revenue due to a change to previously recorded estimates of tickets expected to spoil in the future, which impacted second quarter 2015 year-over-year unit revenue comparisons by approximately one percent. Another two to three percent of the </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2015 year-over-year unit revenue decline was driven by a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">4.6</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent increase in average stage length and a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2.4</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent increase in gauge, both as compared with second quarter 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#8220;We continue to be extremely pleased with our development markets in Dallas. They are remarkably strong, surpassing system average margins and returns. In April, we launched nine additional daily nonstop flights, bringing our total daily flights out of Love Field to 166. By August 2015, we are scheduled to operate 180 weekday departures to 50 nonstop destinations.</font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Our international expansion is also progressing, as planned, and producing expected results. We began service to Puerto Vallarta (PVR) in June and announced daily service between PVR and Denver beginning in November 2015, pending foreign government approval. We are excited to begin service by the end of this year between eight international cities and Houston (Hobby), including inaugural service to Belize City, Belize in October 2015, and Liberia, Costa Rica in November 2015, both pending foreign government approvals. </font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Earlier this month, we were delighted to amend and extend our long-standing partnership with Chase for our co-branded credit card agreement. Beginning in third quarter 2015 and continuing thereafter, we expect to realize significant revenue enhancements. Since we re-launched our award-winning frequent flyer program in 2011, we have nearly doubled the size of our program, in terms of membership, and grown our credit card program, proportionately.&#160; </font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"While some yield softness has continued into July, demand thus far remains strong. Based on current bookings and revenue trends, and including the estimated benefit to operating revenues from our amended co-branded credit card agreement, we are currently estimating third quarter 2015 unit revenues to decline a modest one percent from third quarter 2014. Taking into consideration the ongoing impact of increased stage and gauge, as well as 18 percent of our network under development in third quarter 2015, we are very pleased with our third quarter revenue outlook.</font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">"Overall, our network performance is exceptional. For this year, we are growing our ASMs approximately seven percent, year-over-year.&#160;The annualized impact of our 2015 expansion is </font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">expected to contribute the majority of 2016's year-over-year capacity growth. As we continue to optimize our network, we are currently planning to grow our total 2016 ASMs in the five to six percent range, year-over-year, with the goal to sustain strong margins and ROIC levels in line with 2015."</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Financial Results</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The Company's </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;total operating revenues were $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">5.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, a </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">2.0</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent increase compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, largely driven by second quarter 2015 passenger revenues of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$4.9 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. In second quarter 2014, the Company recorded $47 million in additional passenger revenues due to a change to previously recorded estimates of tickets expected to spoil in the future, contributing to the challenging year-over-year comparisons in second quarter 2015 revenue trends.&#160; </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Subsequent to June 30, 2015, the Company executed an amended co-branded credit card agreement with Chase, through which the Company sells loyalty points and other items to Chase. For accounting purposes, the amended agreement materially modifies the previously existing agreement between Chase and the Company and is subject to Accounting Standards Update 2009-13, "Multiple-Deliverable Revenue Arrangements - a consensus of the FASB Emerging Issues Task Force" (ASU 2009-13). The Company currently estimates that the combined impact from the amended agreement and the effect of the change in accounting methodology to ASU 2009-13 will increase its GAAP operating revenues by approximately $400 million in second half 2015, as compared with the same period last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Under the transition provisions of ASU 2009-13, the existing deferred revenue liability will be revalued to reflect the estimated selling price of the undelivered elements of the contract at the date of the amended agreement.&#160;As a result, and included within the estimated increase to GAAP operating revenues of approximately $400 million in second half 2015, the Company expects to record a one-time non-cash reduction to the deferred revenue liability with a corresponding increase to operating revenues in third quarter 2015 of approximately $150 million, which will be recorded as a special revenue item and is, therefore, excluded from the Company's outlook on third quarter 2015 unit revenues. The remaining approximately $250 million estimated benefit will be included in second half 2015 unit revenues. The estimated portion of that amount related to third quarter 2015 was included in the Company's current outlook for a third quarter 2015 unit revenue decline of approximately one percent, year-over-year.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Total operating expenses in </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">decrease</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">d </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">5.0</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;percent to $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">4.0 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, compared with </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2014</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. Excluding special items, operating income was $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.9 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for first half 2015, compared with $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;for first half 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net income for first half 2015 was $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.57</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, compared with $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">617 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">0.88</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, for the same period last year. Excluding special items, net income for first half 2015 was $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.69</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, compared with $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">611 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, or $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">0.87</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;per diluted share, for the same period last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Balance Sheet and Cash Flows</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">As of June 30, 2015, the Company had approximately $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">3.1 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in cash and short-term investments, and a fully available unsecured revolving credit line of $1 billion. Net cash provided by operations during </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">$627 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, capital expenditures were $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">428 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, and assets constructed for others, net of reimbursements, were $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">19 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, resulting in free cash flow</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:7pt">1</sup></font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">180 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">. The Company repaid </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">$40 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in debt and capital lease obligations during </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-decoration:none;">second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, and intends to repay approximately $95 million in debt and capital lease obligations during the remainder of 2015. The Company funded $355 million to its ProfitSharing Plan during second quarter 2015 as a result of its 2014 results. In past years, the Company's annual profitsharing contribution was funded in third quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">During </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">second quarter 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">, the Company returned $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">430 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to its Shareholders through the payment of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">50 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in dividends and the repurchase of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">380 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in common stock. The Company completed its previous $1.0 billion share repurchase program with the repurchase of $80 million in common stock, or 1.9 million shares, during second quarter 2015. On May 13, 2015, the Company's Board of Directors authorized a new $1.5 billion share repurchase program, along with a 25 percent increase in the Company's quarterly dividend. Under the new $1.5 billion share repurchase program, the Company repurchased $300 million in common stock, or 8.1 million shares, pursuant to an accelerated share repurchase (ASR) program launched and completed during the quarter, bringing total shares repurchased during second quarter 2015 to approximately 10 million. In addition, during second quarter 2015, the Company received the remaining 1.8 million shares pursuant to the first quarter 2015 $300 million ASR program, bringing the total shares repurchased under that ASR program to 6.9 million. For first half 2015, free cash flow was a strong $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">1.0 billion</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;which enabled the Company to return $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">811 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;to Shareholders through the payment of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">131 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in dividends and the repurchase of $</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">680 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">&#32;in common stock.&#160;The Company intends to repurchase an additional $500 million of Southwest common stock under an ASR program expected to be launched soon, which would bring total repurchases of common stock in 2015 to nearly $1.2 billion. Subsequent to the launch of the planned $500 million ASR program, the Company will have $700 million remaining under its existing $1.5 billion share repurchase program. </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:232%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Fleet</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">During second quarter 2015, the Company's fleet increased by ten to 689 aircraft at period end. This reflects the second quarter delivery of six new Boeing 737-800s and five pre-owned Boeing 737-700s, as well as the retirement of one Boeing 737 Classic aircraft. The Company continues to manage to roughly 700 aircraft in 2015 and continues to expect to grow its net fleet approximately two percent, year-over-year, in 2016. As an extension of its fleet modernization initiatives, during second quarter 2015, the Company designated its 31 Boeing firm orders in 2016 as 737-800s rather than 737-700s and added 31 pre-owned 737-700 aircraft scheduled for delivery through 2018. In addition, subsequent to June 30, 2015, the Company canceled the 12 737NG options scheduled for delivery in 2016.  Additional information regarding these revisions to the Company's aircraft delivery schedule is included in the accompanying tables.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s3D952711F329DBC41EA4AFF945494ED8"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;text-decoration:underline;">Awards and Recognitions</font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">683</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;"><div style="text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="text-align:center;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">0.9%</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td colspan="2" style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;font-weight:bold;">689</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;"><div style="text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td colspan="2" style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;"><div style="text-align:right;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">683</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;"><div style="text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="overflow:hidden;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#160;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:bottom;padding-left:2px;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;padding-right:2px;"><div style="text-align:center;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">0.9%</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(1) A revenue passenger mile is one paying passenger flown one mile. Also referred to as "traffic," which is a measure of demand for a given period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(2) An available seat mile is one seat (empty or full) flown one mile. Also referred to as "capacity," which is a measure of the space available to carry passengers in a given period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(3) Revenue passenger miles divided by available seat miles.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(4) Seats flown is calculated using total number of seats available by aircraft type multiplied by the total trips flown by the same aircraft type during a particular period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(5) Seats per trip is calculated using seats flown divided by trips flown. Also referred to as &#8220;gauge.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(6) Calculated as passenger revenue divided by revenue passenger miles. Also referred to as "yield," this is the average cost paid by a paying passenger to fly one mile, which is a measure of revenue production and fares.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(7) RASM (unit revenue) - Operating revenue yield per ASM, calculated as operating revenue divided by available seat miles. Also referred to as "operating unit revenues," this is a measure of operating revenue production based on the total available seat miles flown during a particular period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(8) PRASM (Passenger unit revenue) - Passenger revenue yield per ASM, calculated as passenger revenue divided by available seat miles. Also referred to as &#8220;passenger unit revenues,&#8221; this is a measure of passenger revenue production based on the total available seat miles flown during a particular period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;text-align:left;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(9) CASM (unit costs) - Operating expenses per ASM, calculated as operating expenses divided by available seat miles. Also referred to as "unit costs" or "cost per available seat mile," this is the average cost to fly an aircraft seat (empty or full) one mile, which is a measure of cost efficiencies.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:4px;padding-top:4px;font-size:8pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;">(10) Aircraft in the Company's fleet at period end, less Boeing 717-200s removed from service in preparation for transition out of the fleet.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s918D9A41D5E32A294C6BAFF93126C55E"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Southwest Airlines Co.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">Return on Invested Capital (ROIC)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">(See Note Regarding Use of Non-GAAP Financial Measures)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">(in millions)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">(unaudited)</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">(2) The Company has flexibility to substitute MAX 7 in lieu of&#160;MAX 8 firm orders beginning in 2019.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">(3) Includes </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">13</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;737-800s and </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">13</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;737-700s delivered as of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">July&#160;20, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s28629D0B441DE7381E6AAFF946EB36DA"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">NOTE REGARDING USE OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The Company's unaudited consolidated financial statements are prepared in accordance with GAAP. These GAAP financial statements include (i) unrealized non-cash adjustments and reclassifications, which can be significant, as a result of accounting requirements and elections made under accounting pronouncements relating to derivative instruments and hedging and (ii) other charges the Company believes are not indicative of its ongoing operational performance.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">As a result, the Company also provides financial information in this release that was not prepared in accordance with GAAP and should not be considered as an alternative to the information prepared in accordance with GAAP. The Company provides supplemental non-GAAP financial information, including results that it refers to as &#8220;economic,&#8221; which the Company's management utilizes to evaluate its ongoing financial performance and the Company believes provides greater transparency to investors as supplemental information to its GAAP results. The Company's economic financial results differ from GAAP results in that they only include the actual cash settlements from fuel hedge contracts--all reflected within Fuel and oil expense in the period of settlement. Thus, Fuel and oil expense on an economic basis reflects the Company's actual net cash outlays for fuel during the applicable period, inclusive of settled fuel derivative contracts. Any net premium costs paid related to option contracts are reflected as a component of Other (gains) losses, net, for both GAAP and non-GAAP (including economic) purposes in the period of contract settlement. The Company believes these economic results provide a better measure of the impact of the Company's fuel hedges on its operating performance and liquidity since they exclude the unrealized, non-cash adjustments and reclassifications that are recorded in GAAP results in accordance with accounting guidance relating to derivative instruments, and they reflect all cash settlements related to fuel derivative contracts within Fuel and oil expense. This enables the Company's management, as well as investors, to consistently assess the Company's operating performance on a year-over-year or quarter-over-quarter basis after considering all efforts in place to manage fuel expense. However, because these measures are not determined in accordance with GAAP, such measures are susceptible to varying calculations and not all companies calculate the measures in the same manner. As a result, the aforementioned measures, as presented, may not be directly comparable to similarly titled measures presented by other companies.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Further information on (i) the Company's fuel hedging program, (ii) the requirements of accounting for derivative instruments, and (iii) the causes of hedge ineffectiveness and/or mark-to-market gains or losses from derivative instruments is included in the Company's Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended December 31, 2014.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">In addition to its &#8220;economic&#8221; financial measures, as defined above, the Company has also provided other non-GAAP financial measures, including results that it refers to as &#8220;excluding special items,&#8221; as a result of items that the Company believes are not indicative of its ongoing operations. These include expenses associated with the Company's acquisition and integration of AirTran, collective bargaining ratification bonuses for certain workgroups, and a gain resulting from a litigation settlement received in January 2015. The Company believes that evaluation of its financial performance can be enhanced by a presentation of results that exclude the impact of these items in order to evaluate the results on a comparative basis with results in prior periods that do not include such items and as a basis for evaluating operating results in future periods. As a result of the Company's acquisition of AirTran, which closed on May 2, 2011, the Company has incurred substantial charges associated with integration of the two companies. Given that the AirTran integration process has been effectively completed, the Company does not anticipate significant future integration expenditure requirements, but may incur smaller incremental costs associated primarily with the continuing conversion and sublease of the Boeing 717 fleet throughout 2015. While the Company cannot predict the exact timing or amounts of such charges, it does expect to treat the charges as special items in its future presentation of non-GAAP results. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">The Company has also provided free cash flow and ROIC, which are non-GAAP financial measures. The Company believes free cash flow is a meaningful measure because it demonstrates the Company's ability to service its debt, pay dividends and make investments to enhance Shareholder value. Although free cash flow is commonly used as a measure of liquidity, definitions of free cash flow may differ; therefore, the Company is providing an explanation of its calculation for free cash flow. For the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">three months ended</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, the Company generated </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$180 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;in free cash flow, calculated as operating cash flows of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$627 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;less capital expenditures of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$428 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;less assets constructed for others of&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$22 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#160;plus reimbursements for assets constructed for others of&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><br><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s28629D0B441DE7381E6AAFF946EB36DA"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;padding-bottom:8px;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">For the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">six months ended</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">June&#160;30, 2015</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">, the Company generated </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$1,039 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;in free cash flow, calculated as operating cash flows of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$2,079 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;less capital expenditures of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$1,001 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#32;less assets constructed for others of&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$44 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">&#160;plus reimbursements for assets constructed for others of&#160;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">$5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div well the Company generates operating income relative to the capital it has invested in its business.&#160;Although ROIC is commonly used as a measure of capital efficiency, definitions of ROIC may differ; therefore, the Company is providing an explanation of its calculation for ROIC in the accompanying reconciliation tables to the press release (See Return on Invested
